<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    function isIE() {
      const ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
      const msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE ');
      const trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/');

      return msie > 0 || trident > 0;
    }

    if (!isIE()) return;
    const cartSubmitInput = document.createElement('input');
    cartSubmitInput.setAttribute('name', 'checkout');
    cartSubmitInput.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
    document.querySelector('#cart').appendChild(cartSubmitInput);
    document.querySelector('#checkout').addEventListener('click', function (event) {
      document.querySelector('#cart').submit();
    });
  });
</script><!-- BEGIN sections: header-group -->

<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {
    // -------------------------------------   Read More/ Show Less button in collection description

    const readMoreButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.read-more a');
    if (readMoreButtons.length > 0) {
      readMoreButtons.forEach(function (button) {
        button.addEventListener('click', function () {
          let el = this;
          let readMoreWrapper = el.parentElement;
          let collectionDescriptionWrapper = readMoreWrapper.parentElement;
          if (el.textContent.toLowerCase() === 'read more') {
            collectionDescriptionWrapper.style.maxHeight = collectionDescriptionWrapper.scrollHeight + 'px';
            el.textContent = 'Show less';
          } else if (el.textContent.toLowerCase() === 'show less') {
            collectionDescriptionWrapper.style.maxHeight = '48px';
            el.textContent = 'Read more';
          }
        });
      });
    }
  });
</script>

<script>
                        function createSlider () {
                          var slider = document.getElementById('slider');
                          noUiSlider.create(slider, {
                              connect: true,
                              range: {
                                  'min': 0,
                                  'max': 285
                              },
                              step: 1,
                              pips: {
                                  mode: 'range',
                                  density: 100
                              },
                              start: [0, 284.95]
                          });
                          
                          
                          slider.noUiSlider.on('slide', function (values, handle) {
                              document.getElementById('Filter-Price-GTE').value = values[0];
                              document.getElementById('Filter-Price-LTE').value = values[1];

                              var el = document.getElementById('Filter-Price-LTE');
                              el.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', {'bubbles': true}));
                          });
                        }

                        createSlider()

                        document.addEventListener(
                          "section:rendered",
                          (event) => {
                            createSlider()
                          },
                          false
                        );
                      </script>
</div>

<script>
                      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
                        var ulLists = document.querySelectorAll('.ul-list-check-2');

                        ulLists.forEach(function(ulList) {
                          var liCount = ulList.querySelectorAll('li').length;
                          console.log("Number of <li> elements:", liCount);

                          if (liCount === 0) {
                            var disclosureVertical = findDisclosureVertical(ulList);
                            if (disclosureVertical) {
                              disclosureVertical.classList.add('hide_element');
                            }
                          }
                        });

                        // Function to find the corresponding .facets__disclosure-vertical element
                        function findDisclosureVertical(element) {
                          var parent = element.parentElement;
                          while (parent) {
                            if (parent.classList.contains('facets__disclosure-vertical')) {
                              return parent;
                            }
                            parent = parent.parentElement;
                          }
                          return null;
                        }
                      });
                      </script>

<script>
                      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
                        var ulLists = document.querySelectorAll('.ul-list-check-4');

                        ulLists.forEach(function(ulList) {
                          var liCount = ulList.querySelectorAll('li').length;
                          console.log("Number of <li> elements:", liCount);

                          if (liCount === 0) {
                            var disclosureVertical = findDisclosureVertical(ulList);
                            if (disclosureVertical) {
                              disclosureVertical.classList.add('hide_element');
                            }
                          }
                        });

                        // Function to find the corresponding .facets__disclosure-vertical element
                        function findDisclosureVertical(element) {
                          var parent = element.parentElement;
                          while (parent) {
                            if (parent.classList.contains('facets__disclosure-vertical')) {
                              return parent;
                            }
                            parent = parent.parentElement;
                          }
                          return null;
                        }
                      });
                      </script>

<script>
                      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
                        var ulLists = document.querySelectorAll('.ul-list-check-6');

                        ulLists.forEach(function(ulList) {
                          var liCount = ulList.querySelectorAll('li').length;
                          console.log("Number of <li> elements:", liCount);

                          if (liCount === 0) {
                            var disclosureVertical = findDisclosureVertical(ulList);
                            if (disclosureVertical) {
                              disclosureVertical.classList.add('hide_element');
                            }
                          }
                        });

                        // Function to find the corresponding .facets__disclosure-vertical element
                        function findDisclosureVertical(element) {
                          var parent = element.parentElement;
                          while (parent) {
                            if (parent.classList.contains('facets__disclosure-vertical')) {
                              return parent;
                            }
                            parent = parent.parentElement;
                          }
                          return null;
                        }
                      });
                      </script>

<script>
                              function createMobSlider() {
                                var mobileSlider = document.getElementById('mobile-slider');
                                noUiSlider.create(mobileSlider, {
                                  connect: true,
                                  range: {
                                    'min': 0,
                                    'max': 284.95
                                                                },
                              pips: {
                                mode: 'range',
                                  density: 15
                              },
                              start: [0, 284.95]
                                                            });
                              
                              
                              mobileSlider.noUiSlider.on('slide', function (values, handle) {
                                document.getElementById('Mobile-Filter-Price-GTE').value = values[0];
                                document.getElementById('Mobile-Filter-Price-LTE').value = values[1];

                                var el = document.getElementById('Mobile-Filter-Price-LTE');
                                el.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { 'bubbles': true }));
                              });
                                                          }

                              createMobSlider()

                              document.addEventListener(
                                "section:rendered",
                                (event) => {
                                  createMobSlider()
                                },
                                false
                              );
                            </script>

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-facets__checkbox');

    checkboxes.forEach(function(checkbox) {
        checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
            const anyChecked = Array.from(checkboxes).some(function(cb) {
                return cb.checked;
            });

            if (anyChecked) {
                window.scrollTo({
                    top: 0,
                    behavior: 'smooth'
                });
            }
        });
    });
});

<script>
  const selectors = {
    items: '.accordian__item',
    questions: '.accordian__item__question',
    questions_icons: '.accordian__item__question__icon',
    answers: '.accordian__item__answer'
  }
  const items = document.querySelectorAll(selectors.items);

  for (const item of items) {
      const item_question = item.querySelector(selectors.questions);
      const item_answer = item.querySelector(selectors.answers);
      
      item_question.addEventListener('click', function(){
          const item_question_icon = item_question.querySelector(selectors.questions_icons);
          
          // Open toggled accordions
          if (item_answer.style.maxHeight) {
              item_answer.style.maxHeight = null;
              item_question_icon.querySelector('svg').style.transform = ''
          } else {
              item_answer.style.maxHeight = item_answer.scrollHeight + "px";
              item_question_icon.querySelector('svg').style.transform = 'rotate(-180deg)'
          }
          
          // Close all other accordions 
          for (const sub_item of items) {
              const sub_item_question_icons = sub_item.querySelector(selectors.questions_icons);
              const sub_item_answer = sub_item.querySelector(selectors.answers);
              
              if (sub_item != item) {
                  sub_item_answer.style.maxHeight = null;
              }
          }
      });
  }
</script>
</div>
